	/*Code indicating the level of confidentiality assigned by the sender to the 
information following*/
	def simpleElement 786 {
		name = "Security Level Code"
		type = types.ID
		minLength = 2
		maxLength = 2

		identifierValues {
			allowedValue("00", "Company Non-Classified")
			allowedValue("01", "Company Internal Use Only")

	/*Free-form name*/

	/*Code designating the system/method of code structure used for Identification 
Code (67)*/

	/*Code indicating a code from a specific industry code list*/
	def simpleElement 1271 {
		name = "Industry Code"
		type = types.AN
		minLength = 1
		maxLength = 30
	}

		minLength = 1
		maxLength = 10
	}
